<rating>5<//rating><Text>Met with a friend for lunch today, and we tried Cajun Crab Shack in Thousand Oaks off of E Avenida De Los Arboles. I have a fondness for Cajun food, particularly for the style I call "Cajun boil" where all of your food is cooked at the same time so everything takes on a really rich depth of flavor. The best part, is it's generally eaten by hand, without utensils. Cajun Crab Shack delivered with delicious, flavorful seafood that was well cooked, seasoned, and reasonably priced. It's location in Thousand Oaks makes it an ideal spot for families looking for a new kind of place for a dinner out, and business types looking for a lunch spot that's a bit of a break from the local sandwich, burger, or salad spot. Though I do recommend you avoid it if you've got important face-to-face meetings immediately after ;). It gets messy, but that's part of the fun. In the end it is tasty, well prepared seafood, at a good price, with friendly service. I highly recommend trying it, and if you like it, recommend it to your friends.<//Text><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMtYBe5WTyIy8ayufjm4THEdCWfyzwvdUF9wEU1=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pics>< resp>

< Review>
We have been there twice and really enjoyed the food. Nice sized portions and reasonable prices. The calamari tasted fresh, but should have been presented as an appetizer as it was a pretty small portion and didn't come with a side. Adding some fries would help. I probably won't order it again at that price point. I like getting clam chowder with my meal, but $9.00 for a pretty small bowl seems too pricey. They should offer a cup at half that price. We loved the crab cakes! Great taste and a nice light breading. We will be back to try more items!<//Review>

< text>
Yesterday, January 22, 2019 I visited your establishment as a consumer with 2 other black people, my sister and brother-in-law, and we were treated as if we were going to steal. Your female employee followed us everywhere we went. She already put the cup I was going to purchase on the counter and was holding it for me. When we were looking at the items in the front by the door she was standing right by the counter lending us assistance and answering our questions. When I went to the cups area she came over and I asked her which one was the Patriots. She showed me and I said I will take it. She asked if I would like the bigger one and I said yes. She said she will hold it at the counter until I am ready to purchase and I said okay. We walked around the store looking at the apparel. As we were standing by the shirts having general conversation and looking at them she came over and started fixing the clothes on the hangers. I was asking her questions about the sports team because I dont know anything about sports but my fiance love sports and since he proposed the night before I wanted to buy him something that I could put his engagement ring into. I figured I would get him a Patriots cup and put the ring inside and give it to him when we go to dinner tonight January 23, 2019. We just happened to walk into the store because we needed to kill time until my other family members arrived at Lock & Key Social Drinkery. We were celebrating my sister birthday which was January 21st and my engagement. I left this establishment without purchasing anything because of the treatment. Let your employees know not all black people steal and I will not jeopardize my government job. My sister and her husband will not jeopardize their government job either. Treat your customers with respect or maybe you just do not want to provide services to blacks. I spent $290.00 at Lock and Key last night. There were approximately 5 staff in your store in different area unpacking merchandise including her. I will not patronize your store due to her behavior and I will share my experience with everyone in all races on social media. This store does not need to be patronized by anyone who accept all races.<//text>

<Review>A friend of mine recommended me to call them when a little tiny bird was stuck on my window, the woman that helped me was so kind, I believe her name was Susan.
I got  worried that the little bird was stuck because he was unbothered by my two cats and sat there for a really long time before starting to try to flap his wings.
The woman on the phone was very calm and tried to talk me through what to do, when we started to get a plan together he flew away. She took the time to explain to me why the bird may have been stuck and confused, I really appreciated that because when everything turned out to be fine I felt a little silly.

< text>
I found an injured crow at work and was sad to think he/she was going to die if I didn't do anything.  Not knowing what to do, I started googling rescues and found WildCare.  They had instructions on their website on how to handle the situation.  I followed them and brought the bird to them.  They were very friendly, knowledgable and welcoming.  I felt confident that I left the crow in the RIGHT place.  Thank you so very much Wildcare staff.  I'm grateful you were there for the crow and me.  Please donate to their cause.  They are worth it for sure!!<//text>

< review>
Amazing organization that takes care of injured local animals of Marin County with the aim of release back into the environment-  any injured local wild animal , including a mouse, will be accepted - No discrimination here!  üíï  (please do not take your domestic pet to this place- this is for wildlife).  Additionally they offer classes and tours that teach you about the local animals that live around us.   Visit at lunchtime to see the feeding of residents that were unable to be released due to injury.  Great to know a place like this exists.  Also- wild care has a hotline that you can call 24/7 for assistance with any injured animal you may find.  üíïüíïüíï‚ô•Ô∏è.  Also there is plenty of volunteer opportunities here should one be be interested - They also accept donations of $$, foods, meds, etc (see list on website) that they can use for their organization and its mission. üíï‚ù§Ô∏è< /review>

< review>
WildCare is the best wild animal hospital, with really dedicated staff, including the many volunteers who make possible the hard, and very delicate care for orphaned and injured animals!
The couple of times we have taken wild animals here, they take in the patients right away, and visited being so courteous, they gave the patient number in case you want to call and get report in the progress of the animals you helped. And even they ask if you would like to be involved in the return to the wild of the animal after it is ready for!
It is amazing, and we learned about some of the programs and education they do at this place, and that they will be moving to a bigger place to keep with the demand of their wonderful job!
We started to join Family Adventures with Marco Berger, and we have been delighted with his knowledge and the places he has chosen for the adventures. We highly recommend to join this great FREE OUTDOORS adventures!<//review>

< text>
My son and I are Nikon shooters and own the D500 and 200-500mm combo along with a 300PF prime. We've been thinking about upgrading to a full-frame so we rented the new Sony 200-600mm lens and A7R IV body to try them out. We've seen very sharp pictures from this combo online and was excited to try it out. We rented the combo from BorrowLenses for a week over Thanksgiving to make sure we had the time to try it out in all sorts of situations.

When we got the lens and took my first pictures however, the photos were coming out very soft at the long end. After using the lens for a couple days and trying it out with multiple different camera settings it was clear that this lens was not producing anywhere close to the sharpness to what we've seen from others online.

Having spent hundreds of dollars to rent this expensive gear, it was disappointing that a company like Borrowlenses would not take the responsibility to ensure they have sharp copies for renters especially with their high-end gear. Moreover, when I returned the lens and explained the issue they replied a week later saying the lens is within specs and we probably did not know how to use it, which is insulting to say the least.

We've rented from other lens rental places (e.g. LensRentals) in the past and never had a problem getting a good version of the lens or taken care of once you point out an issue. If you still have to rent from Borrowlenses, take your iPad, shoot a few photos and check out the gear thoroughly before you accept the rental.< /text>

I'm putting this review up so people are aware of Borrow Lenses. I did so only to be met with threats of being sued, criminal charges files, etc. Demanding to send their camera back (the one we PURCHASED elsewhere) because they assumed it was theirs.

I told them to contact my attorney because I have no problem with providing proof of purchase. They ultimately reopened the investigation with UPS again only to once again conclude the package was indeed LOST. Thankfully, I purchased warranty in the even the gear is lost, stolen, or damaged which allows me to pay a deductible of the equipment. However, they never bothered to mention it when I told them UPS's results. They still firmly believe that the gear we bought is theirs. However, since UPS lost the package and it was never in my possession, I had to send proof to my bank for a refund I paid to rent the gear.

< Text>
Borrowlenses bases its identity around shipping rental equipment to customers.  The nature of its equipment and customers requires accurate timing and delivery or the service is without point.   However it appears to have no safeguards in place to help ensure customers will receive the equipment they have paid to rent.

The first occasion I rented from Borrowlenses several items in the order were unavailable as they had not arrived at the pickup location.  Borrowlenses did not have a deep enough inventory to offer me even basic alternatives I could use to work around items they had failed to deliver to THEIR OWN LOCATION on time.

On a more recent order I requested delivery of my equipment two full days ahead of my scheduled need for it in order to ensure there was time available to correct errors.  The equipment did not arrive until after my need, a full three days late.  And only arrived at all because I actively when onto a UPS site and corrected their shipping label errors.  No one from Borrowlenses noticed that UPS had failed delivery or took any steps to contact me to let me know delivery information needed correction, even after delivery had failed twice and was now two days late.

Borrowlenses then refused to refund the cost of equipment that I was unable to use and had to source from another vendor.  They offered a partial value credit to my account Borrowlenes account, a remedy far short of any professional standard as it is entirely useless in a professional setting where clients must be billed for charges and credit card statements must be balanced.

A company offering to provide equipment by mail for the time sensitive business of video production must be ready to guarantee delivery or refund cost or will find no place of use amongst any kind of professional.</Text>

< text>
I needed to test out a Fuji X series lens on my X-T1. Since BorrowLenses has been on my radar for about two years now, the decision to utilize their services was an easy one. Especially after they opened a NYC branch for pick-up and drop-offs.

<Name>Jeff Cheng<//Name>< user>
116458210298398008235<//user>
<Rate>3< /Rate>< Text>
Home to Lucky and Ross, among other popular shops, this shopping plaza offers many choices for food, grocery, and shopping.

While parking are aplenty, the layout of the shops does not necessarily encourage shoppers to visit the entire plaza, which I believe many one of the reasons shops tend to open and close fairly regularly, except some of the big names aforementioned. However, even Game Stop couldn't avoid the fate of closing their doors here.

You may be surprised to find that Albertsons actually owns both Safeway and Lucky, but as this is the only Lucky store in the City, in my opinion, it is still worth a visit.  While prices aren't always comparable to Safeway, they carry some unique selection that I just haven't found in any Safeway in the City.</Text>

They also have great sales on meat! My daughter patronizes Massage Deluxe & loves it. The hair salon is great too & they sell higher end products. I really like this "strip mall" in the burbs of San Francisco!<//Text>

< Text>
Nice neighborhood open air mall with ample parking and a wide variety of stores ranging from Petco on the west to Lucky's on the east side. In between many places of various types including a Chipotle, Ross, US Postal Service station, and a Big 5 among them. There is a large Wells Fargo branch near the entry from Sloat. <Gmap_id>0x808f7d9f01fbd9c3:0xeb344f103f8fad40</Gmap_id><review>Don't tell everybody- but the ross here is kick-ass! Great selection, well organized, staff is professional, place is clean, esp the restroom, well organized merchandise (how do they do it ?? ) I'm really impressed b/c in other locations, the store is blasted out and seems like a hopeless train wreck of insurmountable disorganization.

HUGE selection of men's clothes. Shoes were decent- at least in my size (12) there was a great selection of some unique shoes I've not seen other Ross' carry. For instance, I found some great Nautica slip on "Vans" style casual mocassin, some killer Nikes that look like ninja assassin running booties, and a pair of hi top Supra brand shoes that retail $110 going for $35. They have a huge selection of back-packs, esp high end ones going for pretty cheap.

Anyhow, you know what I mean when I say it's a good Ross.

Plenty of parking, there's food options, Noah's being the fastest of food options, I think.. And a large Lucky's grocery is there as well.

It's a bit out of the way, but well worth it if you need to hit Big 5 and Ross, for instance, to prep for a trip or some activity.<//review>< user>
